class="uppercase font-bold text-xs">Threat intelligence</span></span></div><h1 class="mt-11 mb-7 xl:my-7 leading-none" data-cslp="blog_template.blt69693e4e2849e905.en-us.title">China’s “Winnti” Spyder Module</h1><p><span class="text-sm leading-[21px]">by<!-- --> </span><span><a class="underline" id="Security News" href="/en-us/blog/authors/security-news">Security News</a></span></p></header><div class="mb-20 xl:mb-32 -mx-5 lg:mx-0" data-cslp="blog_template.blt69693e4e2849e905.en-us.featured_imageConnection"><img alt="" fetchPriority="high" width="1200" height="500" decoding="async" data-nimg="1" class="lg:mx-auto max-h-[500px] object-cover" style="color:transparent" srcSet="/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.contentstack.io%2Fv3%2Fassets%2Fblt281ecbfc2563bf9b%2Fblt5c17a98e070c8b11%2F6643ed60be829f76be3bd791%2Fsec-news-header-3.png&amp;w=1200&amp;q=75 1x, /_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.contentstack.io%2Fv3%2Fassets%2Fblt281ecbfc2563bf9b%2Fblt5c17a98e070c8b11%2F6643ed60be829f76be3bd791%2Fsec-news-header-3.png&amp;w=3840&amp;q=75 2x" src="/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.contentstack.io%2Fv3%2Fassets%2Fblt281ecbfc2563bf9b%2Fblt5c17a98e070c8b11%2F6643ed60be829f76be3bd791%2Fsec-news-header-3.png&amp;w=3840&amp;q=75"/></div><div class="xl:w-8/12 mx-auto lg:wysiwyg-lg xl:wysiwyg-xl" data-cslp="blog_template.blt69693e4e2849e905.en-us.paragraph"><div class="wysiwyg max-w-none"><p><b>Overview:</b></p>
<div>
<p>SonicWall&#x27;s Capture Labs Threat Research Team, recently captured and evaluated a new malicious sample termed Spyder, from China’s &quot;Winnti&quot; hacking group. This backdoor is written in C++ and designed to run on 64-bit Windows. This module is being used for targeted attacks on information storage systems, collecting information about corrupted devices, executing mischievous payloads, coordinating script execution, and C&amp;C server communication. The module is loaded by the MSDTC system service using a well-known DLL Hijacking method. The function names within the modules export table are related to the exported functions of the apphelp.dll system library.</p>
</div>
<p><b>Static Information &amp; Error Checking Information:</b></p>
<div>
<a href="https://securitynews.sonicwall.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Static_Information.gif"><img src="https://images.contentstack.io/v3/assets/blt281ecbfc2563bf9b/blt27f6e9f782f66765/664551ae8b884a64c0b5829e/Static_Information.gif" alt="" asset_uid="blt27f6e9f782f66765"/></a>
</div>
